 In which they say that this figure is from the 2016 Economic Survey
 17 rajyon main kisaanon kii salanaa ausat aamadani maatr 20,000 he
 That is, the average income of farmers does not exceed Rs
 1300 per month
 kya 2022 main kisaanon kii ausat aamadani 2600 hone vaali he
 That too after four years
 ek sawaal or bhi sarkaar ke krishi mantri khud se twit kar sakate hai, bataa sakate hai ki chaar saalon main kisaanon kii ausat aamadani kitni badi he, isse pataa chal jayega ki ham doguni karne ke lakshya ke kitne kareeb hai

 3 pratishat thi
 But only 3 between 2014 and 2017
 6 pratishat kii hi ausat vruddhi hui he
 The comments krishi arthshaastri ashok gulati ne likhaa he ki agar aay dugani kerani he to kheti ke sector ko 2022-23 tak 13 pratishat kii vruddhi kerani hogi
 This is obviously not possible
 is baar sarkaar nunatam samarthan mulya badhaakar dene kaa daawa kar rahi he, kya kisaanon ko mil rahaa he, kai jagahon se khabaren aa rahi hai ki nahin mil rahaa he

 phir se kisaan dilli aa rahe hai
 On 29 and 30 November at Ramlila Maidan
 ve apni samasyaon par desh kaa dhyaan chaahate hai
 The good thing is that the people of the city are listening to the farmers
 samaj rahe hai
 AIIMS doctors have planned to set up free health camps for farmers
 iske liye aapas main dawaaon ko jamaa kiya ja rahaa he
 Boxes are kept outside the hostel, in which students are asked to give whatever medicine they have so that it can be useful for the farmers
 dow
 Harjit Singh Bhatti has told that a large number of doctors are coming forward for this work
 resident doctoron kii is pahal main aligarh muslim uniwarsity ke resident doctor bhi kisaanon ke liye dilli aa rahe hai
 The All India Kisan Sangharsh Cardination Committee has been formed by joining the organization of 200 farmers and is organizing this march
 kota zile ke hadoti ke baaraa zile kii atru tehsil kaa ek gaanv he narsinghpur
 Urad and soybean crops of many farmers of this village were destroyed
 chah maheene se kisaan beemaa raashi lene ke liye chakkar laga rahe the
 Sometimes going to insurance company, sometimes bank and sometimes agriculture department
 bhagirath sharma ne kaha ki krishi vibhaag ne beemaa company ko teen teen patr bheje ki in kisaanon kii sau fisadi fasal nasht ho gai he
 All the news is being published in the newspapers but even after this insurance money was not received
 yahi nahin kisaanon ne bataaya ki bainkon ne jo premium raashi kaati he wo puri kii puri beemaa company ko nahin pahunchi he
 After deducting the premium of 2000, if the insurance company reached Rs 300, it means there is a big scam
 yahi nahin sabhi kisaanon ke kisaan credit card se beemaa kii raashi to le lee gai magar beemaa company ne yah kah kar lautaa diya ki sabaki fasal kaa beemaa nahin hua he
 4 from Bhagirath Sharma's Kisan Credit Card
 51 acre fasal ke liye 2301 rupee kii premium raashi kaat lee gai
 But when the insurance company was contacted after the soybean and urad crops were destroyed, it was told that Bhagirath Sharma had 4
 51 acre zamin kaa beemaa nahin hua he
 0 only
 4 acre zamin kaa hi beemaa hua he
 The premium is Rs 216 only, not 2301
 kisaan court chale gaye or court ne beemaa company par mukadmaa daayar karne ke aadesh die magar aaj tak kuch nahin hua
 The farmers did not get the amount of insurance
 bhagirath sharma ne ek or baat bataai ki kisaan ne fasal boi he soyabean kii magar bank ne beemaa kaa premium katate hue urad likh diya he
 This has also happened so that the farmers get entangled in all these and the insurance company does not have to pay
 bhagirath ji ne yah bataaya ki pichley saal jo beemaa company zile main thi, wo is saal nahin he
 He has been replaced by a new company
 isi tarah 26 agast 2018 ke bhaskar main ek khabar chhapi he madhya pradesh ke datia se
 In which it is written that even after paying the premium of insurance, 3000 farmers did not get the claim
 aaj hi haryana ke sirsa main kisaan kanjumar court pahunch gaye
 Because the insurance company of about 2000 farmers returned the premium so that the claim amount would not be paid
 akhil bhartiya swaminathan sangharsh samiti ke vikalp pachaar ne iske bare main bataate hue kaha ki yah kaise ho saktaa he ki july 2017 main premium raashi lene ke das maheene ke baad beemaa company premium raashi hi lautaa de, isliye ham upabhokta adaalat gaye hai
 Not only this, in 2017, 68000 farmers in Sirsa district insured cotton
 prati acre ke hisaab se kisaanon ne premium di 500 rupee or sarkaar ne di 1500
 So the premium amount becomes 2000 per acre
 kapaas kii fasal kharaab ho gai
 After several months, when the amount of insurance was not received, the farmers of Sirsa started agitating
 kisi kaa 18000 rupee prati acre beemaa clem tha to kisi kaa 22000
 In total, this amount is 310 crores
 beemaa companiyaan or bainkon ke bich chakkar katate katate kisaan yah khel samaj gaye or pani kii tank par paanch chah kisaan chadh gaye
 Then they got this amount
 kareeb 320 karod kii raashi kisaanon ne le to lee, magar apane dam par
 Even after this, 2000 farmers have still not received the claim amount because the insurance company has returned their premium
 kisaanon ko andolan karnaa padataa he, court main janaa padataa he, rasta jam karnaa padataa he tab jaakar beemaa kii raashi milti he
 On 25 November, news has appeared in Bhaskar that 70 farmers will get the claim of insurance in Ashoknagar district of Madhya Pradesh, that too in 2016, and that too on the order of the consumer court
 kisaanon ne kheti se zyada chitthee patri kar lee, daftaron ke chakkar laga die tab jaakar milane kaa aadesh hua he, abhi mila nahin he
 Not only this, the insurance company that was changed last year changes this year
 yah bhi pataa chalata he ki beemaa company zile main apana pratinidhi nahin rakhte hai

 Know 10 facts related to earthquake: 1
 dharti chaar paraton se bani he- inner kor, outer kor, mental or crust
 The crust and upper mantle are called lithospheres
 lithosphere 50 kilometre kii moti parat hoti he
 These layers are divided into sections and are called tectonical plates
 jab in tectonical platon main halchal tej hoti he to bukamp aata he
 Not only this, the effects of meteors and volcanic eruptions and mine testing and nuclear testing also cause earthquakes
 2
 The largest ever recorded earthquake occurred in Chile on 22 May 1960
 yah 9
 There was an earthquake of 5 magnitude intensity
 3
 The largest earthquake since Chile was recorded in the United States on March 28, 1964
 ye 9
 2 was of Magnitude, greatly affecting the area of prince William Sound, Alaska
 4
 Do you know that before the earthquake there is a strange fragrance in the canals, drains and ponds
 aisa isliye hota he kyonki prithvi ke neeche kii gaisen baahar nikalne lagati hai
 Not only this, the temperature of ground water also increases before earthquake
 5
 Alaska is the state with the highest earthquake and the most seismically active region in the world
 is kshetra main kareeb 7
 0 Magnitude earthquakes occur every year
 yahi nahin 14 saal main ek baar kareeb 8 megnitude or isse zyada tivrata ke bukamp kaa aana aam baat he
 6
 har saal kareeb lakhon bukamp aate hai
 But their intensity is less
 shaayad aapako nahin maaloom hoga ki neshnal arthquek information centre har saal kareeb 20,000 bukamp record karata he jisamen se 100 bukamp aise hote hai jinase nuksaan hota he
 7
 shaayad aap nahin jaanate honge ki bukamp kuch second yaa kuch minute tak rahata he
 But the longest earthquake in the history of the Indian Ocean was in 2004
 yah bukamp 10 minute tak rahaa tha
 8
 1556 main shaansi china main aayaa bukamp ab tak kaa sabase bhayanak bukamp tha, jisamen 830,000 log maare gaye the
 9
 bukamp se jo urja nikalati he wo 1945 main japan main daale gaye parmaanu bam se nikali urja se 100 guna zyada hoti he
 10
 bukamp kii tivrata maapne vaale richter scale kaa vikaas america vaigyanik charles richter ne 1935 main kiya tha
 Each next unit on the Richter scale has 10 times more intensity than the previous unit
 is scale par 2

 We will also return on good days
 
 
 lekin kab, or kaise, iskaa jawaab kisi ke paas nahin
 
 
 Now the biggest question is what are the options for the Congress
 
 
 kya priyanka gandhi hi sab marzon kii dawa hai yaa bijepi kii tarah kisi jamini netaa ko congress tarjeeh degi
 
 
 The crisis is that the Congress has no Muslim face, which is acceptable
 
 
 yahi haal dalit, brahman or pichhadi jati ko lekar he
 
 
 Will the Congress try to look beyond Rahul Gandhi in such a situation or will he wait for some divine miracle
 
 
 congress ne loksabhaa or rajyasabha main gaiyr-gandhi ko kaman dekar ek acchhee shuruyaat kii he, or ise kitna aage tak lagu kiya jayega, isi par congress kaa bhavishya nirbhar karegaa
 
 
 The Bombay High Court on Monday directed the Central Board of Film Certification to approve the film 'udta Punjab' with just one cut
 film ke sah-nirmaataa anuraag kashyap ne adaalat ke is faisle kaa swaagat kiya he or kaha ki 'is mudde par hamaara rukh sahi siddh hua
 ' is maamle kii sunwaayee karte hue justise essi dharmadhikari or justise shalini pansaalkar-joshi kii khandpeeth ne sensor board ko film ke liye 'e' pramaan-patr jari karne kaa bhi aadesh diya he
 The film is to be released on this Friday, 17 June
 bombai hoicourt main mukadmaa darj karaane vaale film nirmaataaon ke vakil ne kaha, 'adaalat ne sibiefasi kii punarikshan samiti kii 13 cat kii maang ko khaarij kar diya he or ek cat ke saath film ko paas kar diya he
 In the scene which has been taken out of the film, the hero is shown publicly urinating, which we had already agreed to remove from the film
 ' Earlier, the High Court had said that it did not appear to question Indian sovereignty or integrity anywhere in the film "udta Punjab"
 hoicourt ne kaha, "hamane puri script ye jaanane ke liye padhi ki kya film nashe ko badhaava detii he yaa nahin
 We found that the film does not appear to question Indian sovereignty or integrity through the name of a city or state, or by any indication
 " yah kehete hue court ne kaha ki jab tak ki rachanaatmak swatantraaa kaa durupyog na ho, kisi ko dakhal nahin dena chahie
 The comments court ne kaha ki hamen film main aisa kuch nahin najar aayaa jo punjab kii galat chhavi pesh karata ho yaa bharat kii samprabhutaa yaa akhandta ko prabhavit karata ho jaisaa ki sibiefasi ne daawa kiya he
 The court said on the controversy related to this film, CBFC does not have the right to censor films according to the law as the word censor is not included in the Cinematograph Act
 vaise 'udata punjab' main kuch cat lag sakate hai
 The Bombay High Court does not agree with the arguments made in favor of the abuses used in the film
 gauratlab he ki shuukravaar ko hi hoicourt ne sensor board ke pramukh pehlaaj nihlani ko yaad dilaayaa tha ki unka kaam filmon ko praaanpatr dena he na ki unamem kaat-chhaant karnaa
 Nihalani had scissored 89 scenes of the film before giving the certificate to Anurag Kashyap's "udta Punjab", after which Kashyap and his Phantom Films took the case to court
 "udata punjab" aagaamee 17 june ko pradarshit hone ja rahi he
 While hearing the matter, a division bench of Justice SC Dharmadhikari and Justice Shalini pansalkar-joshi has also ordered the Censor Board to issue an 'A' certificate for the film
 yah film isi shuukravaar 17 june ko relies honi he
 The counsel for the filmmakers who filed the case in the Bombay High Court said, "the court has rejected the cbfc's review committee's demand for 13 cuts and passed the film with one cut
" jis seen ko film se nikaala gaya he, usamen hero saarvajanik rup se peshaab karata dikhaaya gaya he, jise film se nikaalane ke liye ham pehle hi taiyaar ho gaye the
 ' isse pehle, hoicourt ne kaha tha ki use film "udata punjab" main kahin bhi bhartiya samprabhutaa yaa akhandta par sawaal uthta nahin dikhaai diya
 The High Court said, "we read the entire script to know whether the film promotes intoxication or not
 hamane ye paaya ki film kisi shahar yaa rajya ke naam, yaa phir kisi sanket ke madhyam se bhartiya samprabhutaa yaa akhandta par sawaal uthaati nahin dikhaai detii he
 "saying this, the court said that unless creative freedom is misused, no one should interfere
 tippaniyan The court said that we did not see anything in the film that portrayed a false image of Punjab or affected India's sovereignty or integrity as claimed by the CBFC
 court ne is film se jude vivaad par kaha, sibiefasi ko kanoon ke hisaab se filmon ko sensor karne kaa adhikaar nahin he kyonki sensor shabd cinematograph adhinium main shaamil nahin kiya gaya he
 By the way, there may be some cuts in 'udta Punjab'
 film main istemaal gaaliyon ke paksh main di gai daleelon se bambe hoicourt sahamat nahin he
 It is worth mentioning that on Friday itself, the High Court had reminded the censor board chief Pahlaj Nihalani that his job is to give certificates to the films and not to cut them
 nihlani ne anuraag kashyap kii film "udata punjab" ko praaanpatr dene se pehle film ke 89 drishyon par kanchi chalaa di thi, jiske baad kashyap or unki phantum filmas maamle ko court le gaye the
 "udta Punjab" is going to be released on 17 June
